\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02556}02556 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}    \textcolor{comment}{! getTranGaus    Pseudorandom numbers from a truncated Gaussian distribution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02557}02557     \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02558}02558     \textcolor{comment}{!   X = getTranGaus(lowerLim,B) returns a pseudorandom variable generated from a normal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02559}02559     \textcolor{comment}{!   distribution with mean zero and standard deviation one (i.e. standard}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02560}02560     \textcolor{comment}{!   normal distribution) truncated to the interval [lowerLim,B].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02561}02561     \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02562}02562     \textcolor{comment}{!   X = getTranGaus(lowerLim,B,avg,std) returns a pseudorandom variable generated from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02563}02563     \textcolor{comment}{!   a normal distribution with mean avg and standard deviation std}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02564}02564     \textcolor{comment}{!   truncated to the interval [lowerLim,B].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02565}02565     \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02566}02566     \textcolor{comment}{!   [X,P] = getTranGaus(...) also returns the vector of probabilities of X.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{TranGaus__mod_8f90_source_l02567}02567     \textcolor{comment}{!}}
